    )

    def triton_(in_ptr0, in_ptr1, in_ptr2, in_ptr3, in_ptr4, out_ptr0, xnumel, XBLOCK : tl.constexpr):

        x0 = xindex % 768

        tmp1 = tl.load(in_ptr1 + (x1), None, eviction_policy='evict_last')

        tmp6 = 1e-12

        tmp9 = tmp2 * tmp8
        tmp11 = tmp9 * tmp10
        tmp13 = tmp11 + tmp12
        tl.store(out_ptr0 + (x2), tmp13, None)
